add_namespace = alash


country_event = {
	id = alash.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event alash.1" }
	title = alash.1.t
	desc = alash.1.d
	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_ALO_alash
	option = {
		name = alash.1.a
		country_event = {
			id = alash.899
			days = 1
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = alash.1001
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event alash.1001" }
	title = alash.1001.t
	desc = alash.1001.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_war_with = var:219.owner
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_ALO_parliament

	option = {
		name = alash.1001.a
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = var:current_party_ideology_group
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
					election_frequency = 12
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = alash.1000
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event alash.1000" }
	immediate = { 
		hidden_effect = { 
			end_coalition = yes
			clr_country_flag = ALO_elections_ongoing		
			ALO_run_election = yes
			set_country_flag = { flag = ALO_show_deputies_comparison value = 1 days = 30 }
		} 
	}
	title = alash.1000.t
	desc = alash.1000.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = ALO_political_crisis
			has_war_with = var:219.owner
		}		
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_ALO_parliament

	option = {
		name = alash.1000.a
		trigger = { has_country_flag = ALO_ELECTION_USH_ZHUS_VICTORY }
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = radical_socialist
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
					election_frequency = 60
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = {
			ALO_Muqan_Aitpenov_hog_rso
			ALO_Uzaqbay_Qulymbetov_for_rso
			ALO_Torsanov_Qaziy_eco_rso
			ALO_Abilkair_Dosov_sec_rso
		}
		set_variable = { ALO_ush_zhus_deputies_support = ALO_ush_zhus_deputies }
		ALO_calculate_support = yes
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = ALO_Ush_Jus_Victory }
			}
			complete_national_focus = ALO_Ush_Jus_Victory
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = alash.1000.b
		trigger = { has_country_flag = ALO_ELECTION_ZHAS_AZAMAT_VICTORY }

					elections_allowed = yes

			}

		}
		remove_all_ministers = yes		
		add_ideas = {
			ALO_Smagul_Sadvakasov_hog_sde
			ALO_Omar_Almasov_for_sde

		}

			name = "Smagul Säduaqasov"
			desc = "POLITICS_SMAGUL_SADUAQASOV_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/ALO/Portrait_ALO_Smagul_Saduakasov.png"
			expire = "1.1.1"
			ideology = socdem_radical_progressivism_subtype 
		}
		set_variable = { ALO_zhas_azamat_deputies_support = ALO_zhas_azamat_deputies }		
		ALO_calculate_support = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = ALO_birlik_established }
			add_synd_to_coalition = yes
		}
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = ALO_Zhas_Azamat_Victory }
			}
			complete_national_focus = ALO_Zhas_Azamat_Victory
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = alash.1000.c
		trigger = { 
			has_country_flag = ALO_ELECTION_AZAT_VICTORY

		}

				}

country_event = {
	id = alash.999
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event alash.999" }
	title = alash.999.t
	desc = {
		text = alash.999.d
		trigger = { ALO_alash_party_in_power = yes }
	}
	desc = {
		text = alash.999.d2
		trigger = { ALO_alash_party_in_power = no }
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = { 
			has_country_flag = ALO_alash_party_ended
			has_country_flag = ALO_alash_party_secured
			has_country_flag = ALO_azat_party_established
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_ALO_azat
	
	option = {
		name = alash.999.a
		trigger = { ALO_alash_party_in_power = yes }
		set_country_flag = ALO_azat_party_established
		clr_country_flag = ALO_1936_Dosmukhamedov_Dulatov
		set_country_flag = ALO_1936_Dosmukhamedov_Socdem
		hidden_effect = {
			406 = {
				add_to_variable = { ALO_state_azat_pop = ALO_state_zhas_azamat_pop }
				set_variable = { ALO_state_zhas_azamat_pop = 0 }
				add_to_variable = { ALO_state_azat_temp_pop = ALO_state_zhas_azamat_temp_pop }
				set_variable = { ALO_state_zhas_azamat_temp_pop = 0 }
				ALO_get_final_popularities = yes
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { azat_pop = 5 }
		set_temp_variable = { zhas_azamat_pop = 5 }
		every_owned_state = {
			if = {
				limit = { state = 406 }
				ALO_azat_pop = yes
			}
			else = {
				ALO_zhas_azamat_pop = yes 
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = -0.06
		}
		ALO_bop_yermekov_medium = yes		
		set_temp_variable = { party_support = ALO_azat_deputies }
		multiply_temp_variable = { party_support = -1 }
		ALO_change_azat_support = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = ALO_Khalel_Dosmuhamedov_for_sli }
			remove_ideas = ALO_Khalel_Dosmuhamedov_for_sli
			if = {
				limit = { ALO_yermekov_in_power = yes }
				add_ideas = ALO_Aydarkhan_Turlybaev_for_mli
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ALO_dulatov_in_power = yes }
				add_ideas = ALO_Ahmet_Beremzhanov_for_sli
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				ALO_alash_right_independent = yes
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = zhanar_faction_banned
					has_country_flag = alash_faction_banned
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = ALO_alash_party_secured	
			set_country_flag = azat_faction_banned
			set_country_flag = national_faction_banned
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = ALO_wounds_of_alash }
				remove_ideas = ALO_wounds_of_alash
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ALO_modernization_dynamic_modifier } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = ALO_modernization_remove_pp_cost
				set_variable = { ALO_modernization_political_power_cost = 0 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			ORE = {
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = market_liberal
					name = ALO_social_liberal_party2
					long_name = ALO_social_liberal_party2_long
				}
			}
			URL = {
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = social_democrat
					name = ALO_socdem_party
					long_name = ALO_socdem_party_long
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = social_liberal
					name = ALO_socdem_party
					long_name = ALO_socdem_party_long
				}
			}
		}		
	}
	option = {
		name = alash.999.b
		trigger = { ALO_alash_party_in_power = no }
		set_country_flag = ALO_azat_party_established
		set_temp_variable = { azat_pop = 5 }
		set_temp_variable = { zhas_azamat_pop = 5 }
		every_owned_state = {
			if = {
				limit = { state = 406 }
				ALO_azat_pop = yes
			}
			else = {
				ALO_zhas_azamat_pop = yes 
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = -0.06
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				ALO_alash_right_independent = yes
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = zhanar_faction_banned
					has_country_flag = alash_faction_banned
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = ALO_alash_party_secured	
			set_country_flag = azat_faction_banned
			set_country_flag = national_faction_banned
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = ALO_wounds_of_alash }
				remove_ideas = ALO_wounds_of_alash
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			ORE = {
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = market_liberal
					name = ALO_social_liberal_party2
					long_name = ALO_social_liberal_party2_long
				}
			}
			URL = {
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = social_democrat
					name = ALO_socdem_party
					long_name = ALO_socdem_party_long
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = social_liberal
					name = ALO_socdem_party
					long_name = ALO_socdem_party_long
				}
			}
		}		
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = alash.998
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event alash.998" }
	title = alash.998.t
	desc = alash.998.d
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = { 
			has_country_flag = ALO_alash_party_ended
			has_country_flag = ALO_alash_party_secured
			has_country_flag = ALO_halyq_party_established
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_ALO_amanjolov

	option = {
		name = alash.998.a
		set_country_flag = ALO_halyq_party_established
		ALO_bop_dulatuly_medium = yes		
		set_temp_variable = { party_support = ALO_national_deputies }
		multiply_temp_variable = { party_support = -1 }
		ALO_change_national_support = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				set_temp_variable = { coalition_target = token:social_conservative }
				has_coalition_with_target = yes
			}
			remove_soccon_from_coalition = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				set_temp_variable = { coalition_target = token:authoritarian_democrat }
				has_coalition_with_target = yes
			}
			remove_authdem_from_coalition = yes
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			name = ALO_nationalist_party
			long_name = ALO_nationalist_party_long
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			name = ALO_nationalist_party
			long_name = ALO_nationalist_party_long
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				ALO_alash_left_independent = yes
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = zhanar_faction_banned
					has_country_flag = alash_faction_banned
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = ALO_alash_party_secured	
			set_country_flag = azat_faction_banned
			set_country_flag = national_faction_banned
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = ALO_wounds_of_alash }
				remove_ideas = ALO_wounds_of_alash
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ALO_modernization_dynamic_modifier } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = ALO_modernization_remove_pp_cost
				set_variable = { ALO_modernization_political_power_cost = 0 }
			}
		}		
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = alash.997
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event alash.997" }
	title = alash.997.t
	desc = alash.997.d

		set_party_name = {

				}
			}

				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				name = ALO_nationalist_party
				long_name = ALO_nationalist_party_long
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ALO_yermekov_in_power = yes }
			set_temp_variable = { party_support = ALO_zhanar_deputies }

			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = alash.986
					days = 2
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { party_support = ALO_national_deputies }
			multiply_temp_variable = { party_support = -1 }
			ALO_change_national_support = yes			
			set_temp_variable = { party_support = ALO_alash_deputies }
			multiply_temp_variable = { party_support = -1 }
			ALO_change_alash_support = yes			
		}		
		set_country_flag = ALO_bop_ended
		remove_power_balance = { id = ALO_power_balance }
		hidden_effect = {
			KYR = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_government = social_democrat }
					country_event = kyr.13
				}
				else = {
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = social_democrat
						name = ALO_market_liberal_party2
						long_name = KYR_social_democrat_party2_long
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

				popularity = -0.06

					set_party_name = {
						ideology = market_liberal

					}
				}
			}

				set_temp_variable = { ALO_loyalty_change = ALO_azat_loyalty }
				ALO_change_azat_loyalty = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { ALO_zhanar_loyalty < 4 } }
				set_temp_variable = { ALO_loyalty_change = ALO_zhanar_loyalty }
				ALO_change_zhanar_loyalty = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { ALO_alash_loyalty < 4 } }
				set_temp_variable = { ALO_loyalty_change = ALO_alash_loyalty }
				ALO_change_alash_loyalty = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { ALO_national_loyalty < 4 } }
				set_temp_variable = { ALO_loyalty_change = ALO_national_loyalty }
				ALO_change_national_loyalty = yes
			}
			ALO_calculate_alash_party_unity = yes
		}

country_event = { # Jas Azamat
	id = alash.1287
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event alash.1287" }
	title = alash.1287.t
	desc = alash.1287.d
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		ALO_jas_azamat_in_power = yes
		NOT = { 
			has_country_flag = ALO_alash_party_ended
			has_country_flag = ALO_alash_party_secured
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_ALO_alash
	
	option = {
		name = alash.1287.a
		set_country_flag = ALO_alash_party_secured	
		set_country_flag = ALO_alash_party_reorganized
		set_country_flag = ALO_bop_ended
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = zhanar_faction_banned
			set_country_flag = azat_faction_banned
			set_country_flag = national_faction_banned
			every_owned_state = {
				ALO_get_final_popularities = yes
				add_to_variable = { ALO_state_alash_pop = ALO_state_zhanar_pop }
				set_variable = { ALO_state_zhanar_pop = 0 }
				set_variable = { ALO_state_zhanar_temp_pop = 0 }
				if = {
					limit = { 
						ROOT = { ALO_alash_right_independent = no }
					}
					add_to_variable = { ALO_state_alash_pop = ALO_state_national_pop }
					set_variable = { ALO_state_national_pop = 0 }
					set_variable = { ALO_state_national_temp_pop = 0 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 
						ROOT = { ALO_alash_left_independent = no }
					}
					add_to_variable = { ALO_state_alash_pop = ALO_state_azat_pop }
					set_variable = { ALO_state_azat_pop = 0 }
					set_variable = { ALO_state_azat_temp_pop = 0 }
				}
				ALO_set_new_popularities_after_election = yes
			}
			# Parliament #
			add_to_variable = { ALO_alash_deputies = ALO_zhanar_deputies }
			set_variable = { ALO_zhanar_deputies = 0 }
			set_variable = { ALO_zhanar_deputies_support = 0 }
			if = {
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { ALO_alash_right_independent = no }
				}
				add_to_variable = { ALO_alash_deputies = ALO_national_deputies }
				set_variable = { ALO_national_deputies = 0 }
				set_variable = { ALO_national_deputies_support = 0 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { ALO_alash_left_independent = no }
				}
				add_to_variable = { ALO_alash_deputies = ALO_azat_deputies }
				set_variable = { ALO_azat_deputies = 0 }
				set_variable = { ALO_azat_deputies_support = 0 }
			}
			# Popularities #
			if = {
				limit = { 
					ROOT = { ALO_alash_right_independent = no }
				}					
				set_temp_variable = { ALO_new_marlib = party_popularity_100@market_liberal }
				add_to_temp_variable = { ALO_new_marlib = party_popularity_100@social_liberal  }
				add_to_temp_variable = { ALO_new_marlib = party_popularity_100@social_conservative  }
				add_to_temp_variable = { ALO_new_marlib = party_popularity_100@authoritarian_democrat  }

				set_temp_variable = { sum = 100 }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@totalist }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@syndicalist }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@radical_socialist }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_democrat }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = ALO_new_marlib }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@paternal_autocrat }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@national_populist }

				add_to_temp_variable = { ALO_new_marlib = sum } #avoid rounding errors

				set_popularities = {
					totalist = party_popularity_100@totalist
					syndicalist = party_popularity_100@syndicalist
					radical_socialist = party_popularity_100@radical_socialist
					social_democrat = party_popularity_100@social_democrat
					social_liberal = 0
					market_liberal = ALO_new_marlib
					social_conservative = 0
					authoritarian_democrat = 0
					paternal_autocrat = party_popularity_100@paternal_autocrat
					national_populist = party_popularity_100@national_populist
				}
			}
			else = {
				
				set_temp_variable = { ALO_new_marlib = party_popularity_100@social_liberal }
				add_to_temp_variable = { ALO_new_marlib = party_popularity_100@market_liberal  }

				set_temp_variable = { sum = 100 }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@totalist }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@syndicalist }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@radical_socialist }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_democrat }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = ALO_new_marlib }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_conservative }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@authoritarian_democrat }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@paternal_autocrat }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@national_populist }

				add_to_temp_variable = { ALO_new_marlib = sum } #avoid rounding errors

				set_popularities = {
					totalist = party_popularity_100@totalist
					syndicalist = party_popularity_100@syndicalist
					radical_socialist = party_popularity_100@radical_socialist
					social_democrat = party_popularity_100@social_democrat
					social_liberal = 0
					market_liberal = ALO_new_marlib
					social_conservative = party_popularity_100@social_conservative
					authoritarian_democrat = party_popularity_100@authoritarian_democrat
					paternal_autocrat = party_popularity_100@paternal_autocrat
					national_populist = party_popularity_100@national_populist
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ALO_alash_right_independent = no }
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = social_conservative
					name = ALO_market_liberal_party
					long_name = ALO_alash_party_long
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat
					name = ALO_market_liberal_party
					long_name = ALO_alash_party_long
				}
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				name = ALO_market_liberal_party
				long_name = ALO_alash_party_long
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				name = ALO_market_liberal_party
				long_name = ALO_alash_party_long
			}
		}
		ALO_calculate_support = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { ALO_alash_deputies > ALO_total_support }
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = ALO_jas_azamat_ally_azat
					has_country_flag = ALO_jas_azamat_ally_janar
					has_country_flag = ALO_jas_azamat_ally_alash
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = alash.1286
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

		clr_country_flag = ALO_negotiations_with_dutov_success
		set_temp_variable = { party_support = ALO_cossack_deputies }
		multiply_temp_variable = { party_support = -1 }
		ALO_change_cossack_support = yes

			limit = { has_idea = ALO_cossack_autonomy }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = ALO_cossack_autonomy
				add_idea = ALO_cossack_garrison
			}
		}		
		ALO = {
			every_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_trait = RUS_orenburg_cossack }
				set_nationality = ORE
			}
			every_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_trait = RUS_ural_cossack }
				set_nationality = URL
			}
		}
		1208 = { 
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ALO_orenburg_autonomy } }
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ALO_orenburg_autonomy }
					ALO_install_cossack_host = yes
				}
			}
			set_demilitarized_zone = yes
		}
		406 = { 
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ALO_uralsk_autonomy } }
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ALO_uralsk_autonomy }
					ALO_install_cossack_host = yes
				}
			}
			set_demilitarized_zone = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		delete_unit_template_and_units = {
			division_template = "Oral Kazak Diviziasy"
			disband = yes #will refund equipment and manpower
		}
		delete_unit_template_and_units = {
			division_template = "Orynbor Kazak Diviziasy"
			disband = yes #will refund equipment and manpower
		}
		activate_mission = ALO_deal_with_orenburg_uralsk_unrest
	}
}

					irregular_cavalry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
				}
				is_locked = yes
			}
		}	
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_template = "Orynbor Kazak Diviziasy" }
			}
			division_template = {
				name = "Orynbor Kazak Diviziasy"
				division_names_group = ALO_CAV_02
				regiments = {
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					irregular_cavalry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
				}
				is_locked = yes
			}		
		}		
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = { state = 1208 }
			create_unit = {
				division = "division_template = \"Orynbor Kazak Diviziasy\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
				owner = ROOT
				count = 2
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = { state = 406 }
			create_unit = {
				division = "division_template = \"Oral Kazak Diviziasy\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
				owner = ROOT
				count = 2
			}
		}
		ORE = {
			every_unit_leader = {
				set_unit_leader_flag = ORE_original_leader
				set_nationality = ALO
			}
		}
		URL = {
			every_unit_leader = {
				set_unit_leader_flag = URL_original_leader
				set_nationality = ALO
			}
		}
		remove_ideas_with_trait = chief_of_staff
		add_ideas = ORE_Aleksandr_Dutov_carm_pau
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = alash.582
				days = 10
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { # 
	id = alash.5970
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event alash.5970" }
	title = alash.597.t
	desc = alash.597.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = ALO_negotiations_with_dutov }
		1208 = { ALO_is_cossack_host = yes }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = alash.597.a
		add_stability = -0.03
		set_temp_variable_to_random = { 
			var = cossack_change
			min = 0.05 
			max = 0.11
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = { state = 1208 }
			ALO_change_cossack_strength = yes 
		}		
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		if = {
			limit = { ALO_yermekov_in_power = yes }
			ALO_bop_dulatuly_large = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { ALO_dulatov_in_power = yes }
			ALO_bop_yermekov_large = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { ruling_party_pop = -5 }
		every_owned_state = { ALO_ruling_party_pop = yes }
		hidden_effect = { decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_5 = yes }
	}
}

				}
			}

				}

			disband = no
		}
		delete_unit_template_and_units = {
			division_template = "Oral Kazak Diviziasy"
			disband = no
		}

	}

		text = alash.431.d3
		trigger = { has_global_flag = RUS_ALO_turkestan_annexation }
	}
	desc = {
		text = alash.431.d4
		trigger = { has_global_flag = RUS_ALO_turkestan_autonomy }
	}
	desc = {
		text = alash.431.d5
		trigger = { 
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = RUS_ALO_turkestan_alone 
				has_global_flag = RUS_ALO_turkestan_alash_majority 
				has_global_flag = RUS_ALO_turkestan_annexation 
				has_global_flag = RUS_ALO_turkestan_autonomy 
			}
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = alash.431.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = RUS_ALO_turkestan_alone }			
			add_political_power = 50
			if = {
				limit = { ALO_yermekov_in_power = no }
				set_temp_variable = { alash_pop = 5 }
				every_other_country = { ALO_alash_pop = yes }
				hidden_effect = {
					add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = 0.05 }
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { ruling_party_pop = 5 }
			every_owned_state = { ALO_ruling_party_pop = yes }
			hidden_effect = { increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_5 = yes }
			ALO_increase_russian_dependence = yes
			turkestan_set_potential_national_government = yes
			turkestan_enable_all_demand_submission_decisions = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = RUS_ALO_turkestan_alash_majority }			
			every_state = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						state = 1278
						state = 585
						state = 712
						state = 1196
						state = 586
					}
				}
				add_claim_by = ALO
			}
			set_temp_variable = { ush_zhus_pop = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { national_pop = 5 }
			every_owned_state = { 
				ALO_ush_zhus_pop = yes 
				ALO_national_pop = yes 
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = 0.05 }
				add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = 0.05 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { can_declare_war_on = TRK }
				activate_targeted_decision = { decision = turkestan_attack_decision target = TRK }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { can_declare_war_on = UZB }
				activate_targeted_decision = { decision = turkestan_attack_decision target = UZB }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { can_declare_war_on = KHI }
				activate_targeted_decision = { decision = turkestan_attack_decision target = KHI }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { can_declare_war_on = KYR }
				activate_targeted_decision = { decision = turkestan_attack_decision target = KYR }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { can_declare_war_on = TAJ }
				activate_targeted_decision = { decision = turkestan_attack_decision target = TAJ }
			}		
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -50
			set_temp_variable = { ruling_party_pop = -5 }
			every_owned_state = { ALO_ruling_party_pop = yes }
			hidden_effect = { decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_5 = yes }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = alash.431.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = RUS_ALO_turkestan_alone 
				has_global_flag = RUS_ALO_turkestan_alash_majority 
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = ALO_should_be_independent
		turkestan_set_potential_national_government = yes
		turkestan_enable_all_demand_submission_decisions = yes
	}	
}

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event alash.1102" }
	title = alash.1102.t
	desc = alash.1102.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes 
	
	option = {
		name = alash.1102.a
		every_state = {
			limit = { 
				region = 221
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = ROOT }
				remove_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { is_faction_leader = yes } }
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = FROM }
				set_country_flag = was_in_faction_with_RUS
			}
			FROM = { dismantle_faction = yes }
			add_to_faction = FROM
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = was_in_faction_with_RUS }
				ROOT = { add_to_faction = PREV }
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_to_faction = FROM
		}	
		set_faction_name = "Sino-Turkic Prosperity Sphere"			
	}
}

					state = 583
					state = 590
					state = 588
					state = 236
				}
			}
			FROM = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		FROM = {
			clr_country_flag = ALO_IND
			set_country_flag = ALO_RUS
			set_cosmetic_tag = ALO_autonomy
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_ideas = {
					alo_kazakh
					alo_kazakh_0
					alo_kazakh_1
					alo_kazakh_2
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = alash.211
				days = 291
				random_days = 150
			}
		}
	}	
}

country_event = { #Russia Integrates us
	id = alash.101
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event alash.101" }
	title = alash.101.t
	desc = alash.101.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = alash.101.a
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { ALO = { is_ai = no } }
				change_tag_from = ALO
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = PREV
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = { is_core_of = ALO }
					add_core_of = PREV
					if = {
						limit = { has_resistance = yes }
						set_temp_variable = { original_compliance = THIS.compliance }
						set_temp_variable = { original_resistance = THIS.resistance }
						cancel_resistance = yes
					}
					start_resistance = ALO
					if = {
						limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }
						set_compliance = original_compliance
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_variable = original_resistance }
						set_resistance = original_resistance
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = ALO }
			recheck_annexations = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Russia allows us vassalage
	id = alash.102
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event alash.102" }
	title = { text = alash.102.t trigger = { owns_state = 1208 } }
	title = { text = alash.102.t.orenburg trigger = { NOT = { owns_state = 1208 } } }
	desc = { text = alash.102.d trigger = { owns_state = 1208 } }
	desc = { text = alash.102.d.orenburg trigger = { NOT = { owns_state = 1208 } } }

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = alash.102.a
		if = {
			limit = { owns_state = 1208 }
			FROM = { end_puppet = FROM }
		}
		else = {
			add_manpower = 17000 # roughly 10% of Orenburg population
			effect_tooltip = {
				FROM = {
					end_puppet = FROM
					transfer_state = 1208
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # The Submission of the Kazakhs, autonomy edition
	id = alash.104
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event alash.104" }
	title = alash.104.t
	desc = alash.104.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = alash.104.a # Welcome their return.
		effect_tooltip = {
			overlord = {
				annex_country = {
					target = FROM
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			overlord = {
				if = {
					limit = { ALO = { is_ai = no } }
					change_tag_from = ALO
				}
				annex_country = {
					target = PREV
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = { is_core_of = ALO }
					add_core_of = PREV
					if = {
						limit = { has_resistance = yes }
						set_temp_variable = { original_compliance = THIS.compliance }
						set_temp_variable = { original_resistance = THIS.resistance }
						cancel_resistance = yes
					}
					start_resistance = ALO
					if = {
						limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }
						set_compliance = original_compliance
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_variable = original_resistance }
						set_resistance = original_resistance
					}
				}
				add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = ALO }
				recheck_annexations = yes
				add_political_power = 150
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = alash.104.b # THIS IS GOOD
		add_political_power = 150
	}

	option = {
		name = alash.104.c # We need friends, not serfs: you may serve as an independent nation.
		overlord = { end_puppet = PREV }
		add_political_power = 100
	}
}
